		select 
UserId,Email, FirstName,ProfilePicPath,IsEmailVerified,
(select COUNT(pl.Id) from PropertyLike pl JOIN PropertyDetail pd on pd.Id = pl.PropertyDetailId where pl.UserId = @userId)likes,
(select COUNT(po.Id) from PropertyOffer po JOIN PropertyDetail pd on pd.Id = po.PropertyDetailId where po.UserId = @userId)offers,
(select COUNT(pc.Id) from PropertyClaim pc JOIN PropertyDetail pd on pd.Id = pc.PropertyDetailId where pc.OwnerId = @userId)claims,
(select COUNT(ps.Id) from PropertySearchHistory ps JOIN PropertyDetail pd on pd.PropertyId = ps.PropertyId where ps.UserId = @userId and IsDeleted = 0)searches
 from Users Where UserId = @userId
END

	   Update Latitude and Longitude
	   -----------------------------
	   Update PropertyData set Latitude = (CAST(LEFT(LatitudeLongitude, CHARINDEX(',', LatitudeLongitude)-1) As  decimal(30,15))),
	   Longitude = (CAST(RIGHT(LatitudeLongitude, LEN(LatitudeLongitude) - CHARINDEX(',', LatitudeLongitude)-1)  As  decimal(30,15))) 
	   
	   
	INSERT INTO PropertyCrudData(PropertyDetailId,Address,HomebuzzEstimate,Bedrooms,Bathrooms,CarSpace,Landarea,LatitudeLongitude,Latitude,Longitude,BuildingType, Suburb, City)
	SELECT pd.Id,Address,HomebuzzEstimate,Bedrooms,Bathrooms,CarSpace,Landarea,LatitudeLongitude,Latitude,Longitude,BuildingType, Suburb, City
	FROM PropertyData pc Join PropertyDetail pd ON pc.Id = pd.PropertyId
	WHERE Suburb = 'Epsom'
	--AND pd.Id NOT IN (select PropertyDetailId from PropertyCRUDData)
	AND pc.Id NOT IN (Select PropertyId from PropertyDetail)


	INSERT INTO PropertyView
	SELECT 
	PropertyDetailId,52,GETDATE(),NULL 
	FROM PropertyCrudData pc join PropertyDetail pd ON pc.PropertyDetailId = pd.Id
	WHERE Suburb = 'Epsom'
	AND pd.Id NOT IN (select PropertyDetailId from PropertyView)
	   
	   SELECT CAST(SUM(CAST(pd.ViewCount AS float))/COUNT(CAST(pd.ViewCount AS float)) as DECIMAL(10,2)) from PropertyCrudData pc
	INNER JOIN PropertyDetail pd ON pc.PropertyDetailId = pd.id 
	WHERE 
	pc.Bedrooms = 1
	AND pc.Bathrooms = 1
	AND pc.Suburb = 'Epsom'

	SELECT ROUND(CAST(AVG(CAST(pd.ViewCount as DECIMAL(10,2))) AS DECIMAL(10,2)),0) AS SQLAVG   from PropertyCrudData pc
	INNER JOIN PropertyDetail pd ON pc.PropertyDetailId = pd.id 
	WHERE 
	pc.Bedrooms = 1
	AND pc.Bathrooms = 1
	AND pc.Suburb = 'Epsom'
